@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000



### CUSTOM EMPIRES ###
e_abrakhan = {
	color = "abrakhan_black"
	color2 = "abrakhan_gold"
	capital = c_abrashadorh
	definite_form = yes
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				root = character:goldenking1 # The Golden King
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
}

e_isengard_unleashed = {
	color = "black"
	color2 = "white"
	definite_form = yes
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				root = character:6000053 # Saruman
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
	capital = c_isengard
}

k_dunlandkingdom = {
	color = { 247 93 42 }
	color2 = { 220 220 0 }

	capital = c_frecalund
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = culture_group:lotr_dunlending_group
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}
}
